instruction is not counted.

<details>

Tier 1 instructions executed.

<thead>
<tr>

</details>

<td align="right">54.2%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">
Not specialized
<details>

</details>
</td>
<td align="right">27,373,035,696</td>
<td align="right">10.6%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">
Specialized hits
<details>
<summary>ⓘ</summary>

</details>
</td>

<td align="right">34.5%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">

</details>

<td align="right">0.7%</td>
</tr>
